      libstdc++6 \
      qemu-user \
      sed \
      diff \
      wc \
      xargs \
      tar \
      gzip \
      sort \
      head \
      file \
      grep \
      findutils \
      bash \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN wget -O - https://apt.llvm.org/llvm-snapshot.gpg.key | apt-key add - && \
      echo "deb http://apt.llvm.org/jammy/ llvm-toolchain-jammy-16 main" >> /etc/apt/sources.list.d/llvm.list && \
      echo "deb http://apt.llvm.org/jammy/ llvm-toolchain-jammy-19 main" >> /etc/apt/sources.list.d/llvm.list && \
      apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y \
      clang-16 \
      clang++-16 \
      clang-format-16 \
      clangd-16 \
      clang-19 \
      clang++-19 \
      llvm-19 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN add-apt-repository ppa:ubuntu-toolchain-r/test && \
      apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y \
      gcc-13 \
      g++-13 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_lts.x | bash - && \
      apt-get install -y nodejs && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN pip3 install --upgrade pip
  RUN git clone https://github.com/simdjson/simdjson.git /simdjson
  WORKDIR /simdjson
  RUN git clone https://github.com/bloomberg/clang-p2996.git /tmp/clang-p2996 && \
      cd /tmp/clang-p2996 && \
      git checkout p2996
  RUN wget https://github.com/emscripten-core/emsdk/archive/refs/heads/main.zip -O /tmp/emsdk.zip && \
      unzip /tmp/emsdk.zip -d /opt && \
      mv /opt/emsdk-main /opt/emsdk && \
      cd /opt/emsdk && \
      ./emsdk install latest && \
      ./emsdk activate latest && \
      rm /tmp/emsdk.zip
  ENV PATH="/opt/emsdk:/opt/emsdk/upstream/emscripten:${PATH}"
  RUN mkdir -p /simdjson/build && \
      cd /simdjson/build && \
      cmake .. -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release -GNinja && \
      ninja
  ENV CC=gcc
  ENV CXX=g++
  ENV CMAKE_PREFIX_PATH=/simdjson/build
  ENV LD_LIBRARY_PATH=/simdjson/build:${LD_LIBRARY_PATH}
  WORKDIR /simdjson
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

NEXT:
  current progress
  The Dockerfile build failed due to package conflicts in Ubuntu 22.04. The error shows that libunwind-14-dev conflicts with libunwind-dev, and python3-clang-13/14 packages have conflicts with python-clang-x.y. The build stopped at the first RUN command that attempts to install all the packages at once.
  next step
  Split the package installation into multiple RUN commands to avoid conflicts. First, remove conflicting packages (libunwind-dev, rust-all, linux-tools-generic) from the initial installation. Then, install LLVM/Clang packages separately to avoid version conflicts. Consider using specific package versions or alternative packages that don't conflict in Ubuntu 22.04.

NEXT:
  current progress
  The Dockerfile has been created with Ubuntu 22.04 as the base image and includes most required tools. However, the build failed at the LLVM repository step due to deprecated apt-key usage and potentially missing GPG key setup. The Dockerfile successfully installs GCC versions 9-13, Clang 13-14, CMake, Node.js, and other basic tools, but fails when trying to add LLVM 16 and 19 from the official LLVM repository.
  next step
  Replace the deprecated apt-key command with the modern approach using gpg and signed-by. Modify the LLVM repository setup section to:
  1. Use gpg to download and store the key in /usr/share/keyrings/
  2. Update the repository entries to include the signed-by parameter
  3. Ensure the GPG key is properly downloaded before adding repositories
  4. Consider using the official LLVM installation script or updating to use the correct repository format for Ubuntu 22.04

      gcc-13 \
      g++-13 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_lts.x | bash - && \
      apt-get install -y nodejs && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN pip3 install --upgrade pip
  RUN git clone https://github.com/simdjson/simdjson.git /simdjson
  WORKDIR /simdjson
  RUN git clone https://github.com/bloomberg/clang-p2996.git /tmp/clang-p2996 && \
      cd /tmp/clang-p2996 && \
      git checkout p2996
  RUN wget https://github.com/emscripten-core/emsdk/archive/refs/heads/main.zip -O /tmp/emsdk.zip && \
      unzip /tmp/emsdk.zip -d /opt && \
      mv /opt/emsdk-main /opt/emsdk && \
      cd /opt/emsdk && \
      ./emsdk install latest && \
      ./emsdk activate latest && \
      rm /tmp/emsdk.zip
  ENV PATH="/opt/emsdk:/opt/emsdk/upstream/emscripten:${PATH}"
  RUN mkdir -p /simdjson/build && \
      cd /simdjson/build && \
      cmake .. -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release -GNinja && \
      ninja
  ENV CC=gcc
  ENV CXX=g++
  ENV CMAKE_PREFIX_PATH=/simdjson/build
  ENV LD_LIBRARY_PATH=/simdjson/build:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
  WORKDIR /simdjson
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

NEXT:
  current progress
  The Dockerfile has been created with Ubuntu 22.04 as base, successfully installed basic build tools, GCC versions 9-13, Clang versions 13-14, Node.js, Python3, and various utilities. However, the build failed when attempting to add LLVM 16 and 19 repositories using apt-key (which is deprecated) and installing Clang 16/19.
  next step
  Replace the deprecated apt-key method with the modern approach using signed-by in the repository configuration. Modify the LLVM repository setup section to:
  1. Download the GPG key to /etc/apt/keyrings/
  2. Use signed-by parameter in the repository configuration
  3. Update the repository URLs to use the correct format for Ubuntu 22.04 (jammy)
  4. Consider splitting the LLVM installation into separate RUN commands for better error isolation

NEXT:
  current progress
  The Dockerfile successfully installs Ubuntu 22.04 base packages, GCC compilers (9-13), Clang compilers (13-14), Node.js, Python3, and various build tools. It also sets up LLVM APT repositories for Clang 16 and 19. However, the build fails when trying to install Clang 16 and 19 packages, likely because the packages are not available in the repositories or there's a dependency conflict.
  next step
  Remove the installation of Clang 19 and LLVM 19 from the Dockerfile since they may not be available in the Ubuntu 22.04 repositories. Keep only Clang 16 installation, or alternatively, check if the LLVM repository is properly configured and accessible before attempting to install these packages.

      cd /opt/emsdk && \
      ./emsdk install latest && \
      ./emsdk activate latest && \
      rm /tmp/emsdk.zip
  ENV PATH="/opt/emsdk:/opt/emsdk/upstream/emscripten:${PATH}"
  RUN mkdir -p /simdjson/build && \
      cd /simdjson/build && \
      cmake .. -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release -GNinja && \
      ninja
  ENV CC=gcc
  ENV CXX=g++
  ENV CMAKE_PREFIX_PATH=/simdjson/build
  ENV LD_LIBRARY_PATH=/simdjson/build:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
  WORKDIR /simdjson
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 7 ---
